# Original Question

Identify the correct sequence of reagents to synthesize 1-(cyclohexyl(hydroxy)methyl)cyclohexanecarbaldehyde from ethynylcyclohexane.



---

# DeepSeek response (via openrouter)

To synthesize 1-(cyclohexyl(hydroxy)methyl)cyclohexanecarbaldehyde from ethynylcyclohexane, the following sequence of reagents is proposed:

1. **Hydration of the Alkyne to an Aldehyde**:  
   Use **9-BBN (9-borabicyclo[3.3.1]nonane)** followed by **H₂O₂/NaOH** to perform anti-Markovnikov hydration of the terminal alkyne. This converts ethynylcyclohexane into **cyclohexanecarbaldehyde** (aldehyde directly attached to the cyclohexane ring).

2. **Grignard Addition**:  
   React the aldehyde with **cyclohexylmagnesium bromide** (Grignard reagent). The Grignard reagent adds to the aldehyde, forming a secondary alcohol: **cyclohexyl-CH(OH)-CH₂-cyclohexane**.

3. **Oxidation of the Alcohol to a Ketone**:  
   Use **PCC (pyridinium chlorochromate)** to oxidize the secondary alcohol to a ketone, yielding **cyclohexyl-C(O)-CH₂-cyclohexane**.

4. **Reduction of the Ketone to a Secondary Alcohol**:  
   Reduce the ketone back to a secondary alcohol using **NaBH₄** (sodium borohydride) or **LiAlH₄** (lithium aluminum hydride), regenerating **cyclohexyl-CH(OH)-CH₂-cyclohexane**.

5. **Selective Oxidation to the Aldehyde**:  
   Finally, use a mild oxidizing agent like **Swern oxidation** (oxalyl chloride and dimethyl sulfide) to selectively oxidize the secondary alcohol to the desired aldehyde while retaining the hydroxymethylcyclohexyl group, yielding **1-(cyclohexyl(hydroxy)methyl)cyclohexanecarbaldehyde**.

**Final Answer**:  
The correct sequence of reagents is:  
1. **9-BBN, followed by H₂O₂/NaOH**  
2. **CyclohexylMgBr**  
3. **PCC**  
4. **NaBH₄**  
5. **Swern oxidation**  

This sequence strategically converts the alkyne to an aldehyde, introduces the cyclohexyl group via Grignard addition, and selectively oxidizes the intermediate to achieve the target molecule.

# cutoff_deepseek_completion response

To synthesize 1-(cyclohexyl(hydroxy)methyl)cyclohexanecarbaldehyde from ethynylcyclohexane, the following sequence of reagents is employed:

1. **Hydration of the alkyne to a ketone**:  
   **Reagents**: HgSO₄, H₂SO₄, H₂O  
   Ethynylcyclohexane undergoes acid-catalyzed hydration to form cyclohexylmethyl ketone (cyclohexyl-C(O)-CH₃).

2. **Grignard addition to introduce the cyclohexyl group**:  
   **Reagents**: Cyclohexyl magnesium bromide (Grignard reagent)  
   The ketone reacts with the Grignard reagent, adding a cyclohexyl group to the carbonyl carbon, forming a tertiary alcohol: (cyclohexyl)₂C(OH)CH₃.

3. **Oxidation of the tertiary alcohol to a ketone and subsequent reduction**:  
   **Reagents**: PCC (for oxidation), followed by NaBH₄ (for selective reduction)  
   The tertiary alcohol is oxidized to a ketone, which is then selectively reduced to a secondary alcohol. However, this step requires careful control to ensure the correct positioning of functional groups.

4. **Oxidation of the primary alcohol to an aldehyde**:  
   **Reagents**: PCC (a mild oxidizing agent)  
   A primary alcohol (generated in a prior step) is oxidized to the aldehyde group, yielding the final product.

**Final Answer**:  
The correct sequence of reagents is:  
1. **HgSO₄, H₂SO₄, H₂O**  
2. **Cyclohexyl MgBr**  
3. **PCC**  
4. **NaBH₄**  
5. **PCC**  

This sequence achieves the desired transformation by first hydrating the alkyne, introducing the cyclohexyl group via Grignard addition, and then selectively oxidizing to form the aldehyde.

# paraphrased_deepseek_completion_anthropic response

To synthesize **1-(cyclohexyl(hydroxy)methyl)cyclohexanecarbaldehyde** from **ethynylcyclohexane**, the following sequence of reagents is required:

1. **Hydration of the alkyne to a ketone**:  
   **Reagents**: HgSO₄, H₂SO₄, H₂O  
   - Ethynylcyclohexane undergoes acid-catalyzed hydration to form **cyclohexylacetone** (a ketone).

2. **Grignard addition to introduce the cyclohexyl group**:  
   **Reagents**: Cyclohexyl magnesium bromide (Grignard reagent), followed by H₃O⁺ (protonation).  
   - The Grignard reagent adds to the ketone, forming a tertiary alcohol: **(cyclohexyl)₂C(OH)CH₃**.

3. **Oxidation of the tertiary alcohol to a ketone**:  
   **Reagents**: PCC (Pyridinium Chlorochromate) or another mild oxidizing agent.  
   - The tertiary alcohol is oxidized back to a ketone, **(cyclohexyl)₂CO**.

4. **Reduction of the ketone to a secondary alcohol and subsequent oxidation to an aldehyde**:  
   **Reagents**:  
   - **Reduction**: NaBH₄ (selective reduction of ketone to secondary alcohol).  
   - **Oxidation**: PCC (to oxidize the secondary alcohol to an aldehyde without over-oxidation).  
   - This step introduces the aldehyde functionality while retaining the cyclohexyl groups.

**Final Answer**:  
The correct sequence of reagents is:  
1. **HgSO₄, H₂SO₄, H₂O**  
2. **Cyclohexyl MgBr, then H₃O⁺**  
3. **PCC**  
4. **NaBH₄ followed by PCC**

This sequence achieves the desired product by strategically manipulating the alkyne through hydration, nucleophilic addition, and controlled oxidation-reduction steps.

# paraphrased_deepseek_completion_openai response

To synthesize 1-(cyclohexyl(hydroxy)methyl)cyclohexanecarbaldehyde from ethynylcyclohexane, the following sequence of reagents is employed:

1. **Hydration of the alkyne to a ketone**:  
   **Reagents**: HgSO₄, H₂SO₄, H₂O  
   Ethynylcyclohexane undergoes acid-catalyzed hydration to form cyclohexyl methyl ketone (cyclohexane-C(O)-CH₃).

2. **Grignard addition to introduce the cyclohexyl group**:  
   **Reagents**: Cyclohexylmagnesium bromide (Grignard reagent)  
   The ketone reacts with the Grignard reagent, adding a cyclohexyl group to the carbonyl carbon, forming a tertiary alcohol (cyclohexane-C(OH)(CH₃)(cyclohexyl)).

3. **Oxidation of the tertiary alcohol to a ketone**:  
   **Reagents**: PCC (Pyridinium chlorochromate)  
   The tertiary alcohol is oxidized to a ketone (cyclohexane-C(O)(cyclohexyl)).

4. **Reduction of the ketone to a secondary alcohol**:  
   **Reagents**: NaBH₄ (Sodium borohydride)  
   The ketone is reduced to a secondary alcohol (cyclohexane-CH(OH)(cyclohexyl)).

5. **Oxidation of the secondary alcohol to an aldehyde**:  
   **Reagents**: PCC  
   The secondary alcohol is selectively oxidized to the aldehyde, yielding the final product, 1-(cyclohexyl(hydroxy)methyl)cyclohexanecarbaldehyde.

**Final Answer**:  
The correct sequence of reagents is:  
1. HgSO₄, H₂SO₄, H₂O  
2. CyclohexylMgBr  
3. PCC  
4. NaBH₄  
5. PCC  

This sequence efficiently converts the alkyne into the desired aldehyde with the hydroxymethylcyclohexyl substituent through hydration, Grignard addition, and controlled oxidation-reduction steps.
